Originally formed in Colombia, but now based in Los Angeles, Palenke Soultribe have claimed a spot in the Latin Alternative music world by putting on energetic shows, releasing musically interesting albums and remixes and always pushing the envelope visually and conceptually. The initial line up was formed by producer/bassist Juan Diego Borda and keyboardist/producer Andres “Popa” Erazo. Drummer Andres Zuluaga has collaborated with PST since 2007 being an active member of the band while he was in the USA. However, PST prefers to work as a collective, inviting guest producers, singers, songwriters and instrumentalists to their shows and to contribute on their albums.\r\n\r\nwww.palenkesoultribe.com\r\nwww.twitter.com/palenke\r\nwww.facebook.com/palenkesoultribefanpage\r\n\r\n-----------------------------\r\n8:30pm  Wave Sleep Wave\r\nHey...What?  http://youtu.be/suf1d0x_4xQ\r\n\r\nWave Sleep Wave is a Brooklyn duo centered around Jerry Adler (The Blam, Flugente) and drummer Yuval Lion (who was also in The Blam, Pink Noise). Mixed and mastered by Blake Morgan, the band's eponymous debut startles and shimmers, darts and dashes, through a bevy of nine tightly-wrapped yet gripping tracks.\r\n\r\nIf it's absolutely necessary to pin a label on what Wave Sleep Wave does, you could call it dreampop. Reduced to its essentials, it's a shimmering, glistening, swirling, jangly, misty vortex of guitar textures over steady drums. Frontman/guitarist Jerry Adler is a one-man orchestra, slowly and methodically building a web of textures, sometimes hypnotic, often symphonically ornate, like a late 80s British version of Jon Brion. Influence-wise, there are a million bands out there who ape the catchy, simple, major-key mid-80s sound that New Order and the Cure made so popular; here, Adler reverts back to a deeper, murkier 80s sound that also offers a nod to Wire and the Cocteau Twins. He first made a mark about ten years ago leading the Blam, the catchy but edgy indie pop band that should have been as popular as the Shins but wasn't; a little later, he took a powerfully lyrical detour into Dylanesque acoustic rock with his Flugente project. What's most impressive about this album is that it appears to be just guitars and drums, with no bass, yet the sonics have a gyroscopic balance. Drummer Yuval Lion keeps things moving along tersely and briskly, for the most part. Fans of the dreampop canon from the Cocteau Twins, to Lush, to My Bloody Valentine, to more obscure bands like Downy Mildew, are going to love this record.\r\n\r\nhttp://www.curbcutrecords.com/WSW/WSW.html\r\n\r\n------------------------\r\nSchpilkas (DJ)\r\nhttp://www.schpilkas.com/2012/\r\n\r\nCasey Dunmore, best known as Schpilkas, is a composer and producer for film, tv and video games. A classically trained multi-instrumentalist, Schpilkas blends influences from classical, rock, hip hop and electronic music to create a hybrid style.\r\n\r\nHis original music production credits include the theme songs for reality TV show Tia & Tamera (Style Network) and the NBA Toronto Raptors. Some of Schpilkas’ featured placements include NIKE’s Vapen Sessions, the movie Our Family Wedding (Fox Searchlight Pictures), One Tree Hill (CW), The City (MTV), Jimmy Kimmel Live (ABC), and video música contiene todos los elementos característicos de la música medio-oriental y mucho de la música GITANA, que hace recordar a EMIR KUSTURICA y a GORAN BREGOVIC, matizados con elementos de HIP-HOP y ANDRÉS CALAMARO, MANU CHAO y FITO PÁEZ ,entre otros.\nEntre 2010 y 2014 han realizado 5 giras en Europa pasando por: Festival BBK Live, Festival Viva La Canción, Festival PortAmérica, Festival Lasem, Festival de cine de Biarritz, Primavera Pro. De ahí nacen las experimentaciones de Nima & Supermads. Una banda que tiene 5 añitos, enfocada en lo psicodélico en el sentido etimológico de la palabra, como reveladora del alma. El estilo cambia una y otra vez con elementos fijos como una batería, un djembe, una voz femenina étnica, una voz masculina con textos, bajo, elementos electrónicos y 2 guitarras. Inspirándose mas que nada en el publico, Nima & Supermads entran en acción en Ibiza y solo cuando la invitación es para salvar el mundo!”\n\nBIENVENIDOS AL CASTILLO, BIENVENIDOS AL IBIZA ROOTS jeudi 10 novembre. \nBienvenue dans la Jungle Montpelliéraine….Une Nuit Zébrée organisée main dans la main avec Montpellier Mediterranée Metropole.\n\n3SOMESISTERS – France\nBalkan Beat Box – From New It's not just a mash-up, it's music made by the citizens of a global culture!  Originally from New York and Tel Aviv, Balkan Beat Box (aka BBB) mixes Balkan brass, earthy bass and hip-hop with electronic effects from the dub. Their concerts are explosive, the singer Tomer Yosef there delivering his texts, sometimes political, with passion and energy. The result is a sound assault which makes no quarter and no surrender possible.
